Florence O

In O

Schust O
moved O
to O

from O

and O

of O

in O
the O
world. O

met O

who O
was O
establishing O
a O
new O
furniture O
company. O
With O
Florence’s O
design O
skills O
and O
Hans’ O
business O
acumen O
and O
salesmanship, O
the O
pair, O
who O
married O
in O

grew O
the O
nascent O
company O
into O
an O
international O
arbiter O
of O
style O
and O

FAQs O
What O
does O
'Made-to-Order' O
mean? O
Made-to-order O
means O
that O
once O
we O
receive O
your O
order, O
it O
gets O
included O
in O
a O
production O
run O
of O
that O
item O
and O
when O
it O
is O
completed, O
it O
ships O
to O
you O
directly. O
This O
reduces O
waste O
(we O
don’t O
overproduce O
inventory O
or O
cut O
into O
materials O
that O
aren’t O
needed), O
and O
keeps O
our O
small, O
hardworking O
team O
organized. O
We O
have O
a O
limited O
number O
of O
people O
on O
our O
team O
and O
a O

workflow, O
so O
we O
are O
only O

to O
produce O
a O
certain O
number O
of O
items O
each O
week O
in O
order O
to O
maintain O
our O

DISAINISTUUDIOSkandinaavialik O
stiilitunnetus, O
puhtad O
ja O
ajatud O
vormid O
on O
kindlasti O
märksõnad, O
mis O
iseloomustavad O
meie O
mööblit. O
Disainiprotsessis O
oleme O
pühendunud O
ja O
põhjalikud O
Näiteks O
Voog O
tugitoolist O
valmistasime O
pea O
poolsada O
prototüüpi, O
kuni O
jõudsime O
vormi- O
ja O
disainitäiuseni, O
mis O
annab O
edasi O
meie O
visiooni. O
Diivanid O
ja O
tugitoolid O
olgu O
ilusad, O
kuid O
sama O
tähtis O
on O
ka O
mööbli O
ergonoomika. O
Iga O
inimene O
on O
erinev O
ja O
samuti O
on O
erinevad O
ka O
inimeste O
istumisharjumused O
ja O
ootused O
mugavusele. O
Mõnele O
sobib O
jäik O
ja O
hästi O
selga O
toetav O
diivan, O
teisele O
jälle O
võimalikult O
pehme O
sohva. O
Seepärast O
on O
hea O
võimalikult O
palju O
diivaneid O
läbi O
istuda O
ja O
leida O
omale O
parim O
lahendus. O
Oot-Oot O
Stuudios O
on O
erinevad O
mudelid O
erinevate O
omadustega. O
Valikust O
leiab O
nii O
pehmeid O
vedrudiivaneid O
kui O
ka O
rõhutatud O
alaseljatoega O
tugitoole. O
Loe O
meist O
rohkem O

How O
Our O
Armchairs O
Are O
Made O
We O
build O
our O
armchairs O
up O
from O
a O
hardwood O
beech O
frame, O
using O
traditional O
methods O
and O
materials. O
With O
hand-tied O
coil-sprung O
seat, O
arms O
and O
back. O
Where O
cushions O
are O
used, O
what O
makes O
them O
so O
comfortable O
is O
the O
high O
down O
content O
(50% O
down, O
50% O
feather O
in O
seat, O
and O
70% O
down, O
30% O
feather O
in O
back). O
The O
down O
gives O
the O
cushions O
lovely O
softness, O
while O
the O
feathers O
provide O
loft O
and O
spring.​ O
Where O
castors O
are O
used, O
they O
have O
been O
individually O
hand-cast O
by O
traditional O
English O
metal O
crafters O
to O
a O
very O
high O
standard, O
and O
a O
variety O
of O
finishes O
can O
be O
achieved. O
We O
use O
the O
antique O
brass O
finish O
as O
standard. O
Where O
legs O
are O
used, O
they O
can O
be O
either O
tapered O
or O
turned O
and O
come O
in O
a O
variety O
of O
woods O
and O
finishes O
(see O
'Leg O
Options' O
tab O
for O
more O
details). O
We O
use O
medium O
oak O
as O
standard. O
All O
of O
our O
furniture O
can O
be O
made O
completely O
bespoke. O
We O
want O
this O
to O
be O
your O
perfect O
armchair, O
so O
if O
you O
want O
it O
a O
bit O
bigger O
or O
smaller, O
softer O
or O
firmer, O
or O
anything O
else O
just O
ask O
we O
will O
do O
our O
best O
to O
accommodate. O
The O
price O
excludes O
fabric. O
If O
you O
need O
some O
help O
finding O
the O
perfect O
fabric, O
let O
us O
know. O

quantities O
for O
standard O
models O
in O

fabric O
are O

in O

For O

and O

ABOUT O
US O
The O
Past O
Perfect O

offers O
an O

of O

colonial O

of O

All O

These O

to O

silently O

to O
you O
of O
a O

era. O
Own O
